<USER_REQUEST>
# Sangam Insurance CRM — Complete Build Prompt

## Overview

A **single-file HTML web CRM** for IBM (Insurance Business Manager) agents at Ambak. IBM agents manage insurance leads end-to-end — from the first call to policy issuance and commission payout. The CRM sits inside Ambak's existing Sangam platform as a dedicated insurance module.

**Users:** IBM Agents (internal Ambak team)
**Primary job:** Convert insurance leads attached to home loan customers into issued policies
**Key insight:** Every customer data point needed for insurance already lives in the Sangam HL CRM — the insurance CRM pulls it rather than re-collecting it.

---

## Tech Stack

- Single-file HTML (no framework, no build step)
- Vanilla JS — all state in memory variables
- Google Fonts: Poppins (400/500/600/700/800)
- No external libraries
- All layout via inline styles on structural elements (prevents CSS class conflicts)
- CSS classes only for reusable component styling (cards, badges, buttons)

---

---

## Key UX Principles

1. **Agent never leaves Sangam** — PB panel slides in, quotes appear inline, payment link sent from same screen
2. **Pre-fill everything possible** — Age, loan amount, customer details all pulled from HL CRM. Agent only fills what's new
3. **Stage-aware actions** — Center content changes based on current stage. Agent always knows what to do next
4. **Results replace inputs** — LP calculator results replace the form in-place. ← Recalculate to go back
5. **Milestone tracker as progress contract** — IBM and customer both know what step they're on. No ambiguity
6. **Section forms on demand** — Customer/Income/Property details accessible but not in the way. Click to view/edit
7. **HL context always visible** — HL lead stage shown in sidebar and meta strip. Insurance journey tied to loan journey
8. **Toast feedback** — Every action confirms with a non-blocking toast (bottom center, 2.6s)
9. **No modals for stage transitions** — Stage moves happen inline, page re-renders with new content
10. **Color as status signal** — Green = done/success, Amber = attention needed, Red = missing/lost, Purple = active/primary

---

## Production Considerations (not yet built)

- Actual Sangam API integration (lead data from backend)
- PolicyBazaar embed or API (currently mocked)
- Real payment link generation (Razorpay/PB gateway)
- Document upload to PolicyBazaar portal
- Real-time activity log sync
- IBM assignment logic
- HL lead search against actual Sangam database
- Commission calculation and payout tracking

PROMPT — REDESIGN PROCESSING & POLICY STAGES

Design the Insurance CRM workflow so that the Processing stage ends at Policy Issuance.

Do NOT include MIS updates, commission tracking, policy sharing, free-look management, or post-issuance activities inside Processing.

The Processing stage should only track activities required to get a policy issued by the insurer.

Once Policy Issued is completed, the lead automatically moves to the Policy stage.

CORE PRINCIPLE

Separate the journey into two distinct phases:

Processing Stage

Goal:

Get the policy issued.

Focus:

Customer
Insurer
PolicyBazaar
IBM Agent

working together to complete insurer requirements.

Policy Stage

Goal:

Manage the issued policy.

Focus:

Policy Delivery

Customer Confirmation

Free Look Tracking

MIS Updates

Commission Tracking

Operational Closure
PROCESSING STAGE

The Processing stage should function as a product-specific milestone tracker.

The UI remains identical across products.

Only the milestones change.

PROCESSING HEADER

Display:

Policy Processing Tracker

Current Product

Selected Insurer

Processing Age

Expected Completion Date

Milestones Completed

Example:

Credit Life

HDFC Life

Processing Age:
4 Days

Expected Completion:
24 Jun 2026

6 / 8 Milestones Complete
TRACKER BEHAVIOR

Use a vertical timeline.

Milestone states:

Completed
Active
Pending
Blocked

Colors:

Green = Completed

Purple = Active

Grey = Pending

Red = Blocked

Only one milestone should be expanded at a time.

The active milestone is automatically expanded.

FINAL UX PRINCIPLE

The Processing stage should answer:

What is preventing policy issuance?

The Policy stage should answer:

Now that the policy is issued, what operational activities remain before closure?

This separation should make the workflow extremely clear for IBM agents and avoid mixing insurer processing activities with post-issuance operational tasks.

<USER_REQUEST>
PROMPT — INSURANCE PRODUCT FINALIZATION WORKFLOW

Redesign the Insurance CRM workflow so that insurance products are NOT finalized during lead creation.

The CRM should support a consultative sales process where IBM agents first understand customer requirements, explore multiple insurance products, generate multiple quotes, and only finalize the product when the customer selects a quote.

The system should treat:

Insurance Lead

and

Insurance Product

as two separate concepts.

A lead represents a customer opportunity.

A product represents the eventual solution selected by the customer.

CORE BUSINESS RULE

At lead creation:

DO NOT lock the lead to:

Loan Protection
Property Insurance
Credit Life
Term Plan

Instead:

Create a generic:

Insurance Lead

linked to the customer and home loan journey.

LEAD CREATION

Capture:

Customer Name

Mobile Number

Linked Home Loan

Lead Source

Assigned IBM Agent

Fulfillment Type

Optional field:

Initial Product Interest

Possible values:

Loan Protection

Property Insurance

Credit Life

Term Plan

Not Sure

This is only a recommendation.

It should never control downstream workflows.

HEADER CHANGES

In the lead detail page replace:

Product:
Loan Protection

with:

Recommended Product:
Loan Protection

Display as an editable chip.

Example:

Recommended Product

Loan Protection
[Change]

Until quote selection, agents should be able to modify this freely.

NEW PRODUCT STATE MODEL

Introduce a product status field.

Stage 1

Lead Created

Display:

Product Status

Not Finalized

Badge:

Draft
Stage 2

Interest Stage

Display:

Recommended Product

Loan Protection

Still editable.

Stage 3

Quote Stage

Display:

Recommended Product

<USER_REQUEST>
 PROMPT — IMPLEMENT INSURANCE CRM STATE MACHINE

Build a complete state machine architecture for the Insurance CRM.

The CRM should not rely on agents manually moving leads between buckets. Instead, agents should only update Status and Sub Status, while the system automatically determines the correct bucket and lead progression.

The architecture should follow:

Bucket (System Controlled)
    ↓
Status (Agent Controlled)
    ↓
Sub Status (Agent Controlled)
CORE PRINCIPLE

Agents should only see:

Status
Sub Status
Remarks
Follow-up Date
Pending With

Agents should never manually select:

New
Contacted
Quote
Processing
Policy
Lost

The CRM should automatically move leads between buckets based on predefined transition rules.

INSURANCE CRM FUNNEL

The insurance funnel should contain only the following system buckets:

New
Contacted
Quote
Processing
Policy
Lost

These buckets power:

Funnel reports
Conversion reports
Aging reports
SLA dashboards
Agent productivity reports
Source performance reports
BUCKET 1 — NEW

Represents leads where meaningful interaction has not yet happened.

Available Statuses
Not Connected
Connected
Not Connected Sub Statuses
Customer Busy
Not Reachable
Invalid Phone Number
Ringing But No Answer
Customer Disconnected Call
Switched Off
Voicemail
Connected Sub Statuses
Customer Responded
Basic Discussion Done
Need Detailed Discussion
State Transition Rules
Connected
→ Automatically move Bucket = Contacted
Auto Lost Rule

If:

3 consecutive Not Connected attempts

then:

Bucket = Lost

Status = Contact Failed

Sub Status = No Response After 3 Attempts
BUCKET 2 — CONTACTED

Customer interaction has started.

Available Statuses
Call Back

Interested

Not Interested
Call Back Sub Statuses
Busy Call Later

Requested Callback

Partial Details Shared

Language Barrier

Need Discussion With Family

Need Discussion With Spouse

Call After Office Hours
Interested Sub Statuses
Need Quote

Need Product Explanation

Compare Options

Need Benefit Illustration
Not Interested Sub Sta
<truncated 3216 bytes>
 Statuses
Policy Copy Uploaded

Completed

Policy Cancelled
Policy Copy Upload

Policy Issued

Allow upload:

PDF

Image

ZIP

Store:

Policy Number

Issue Date

Insurer Name

Policy Copy
Policy Shared

Sub Statuses:

WhatsApp

Customer Downloaded
Free Look Period

Track:

Free Look Start Date

Free Look End Date

Usually:

30 days
Cancellation Branch

If:

Customer Cancels During Free Look

then:

Policy Cancelled

Commission Reversed

Refund Initiated
Completion Rule

After:

MIS Updated

Commission Released

Free Look Expired

mark:

Status = Completed
BUCKET 6 — LOST

Centralized loss bucket.

All exit paths should terminate here.

Lost Statuses

REPORTING REQUIREMENTS

Every lead should maintain:

Final Product

Final Insurer

This state machine should become the single source of truth for all CRM workflows, dashboards, reports, filters, automations, SLA monitoring, lead aging analysis, and conversion tracking across Property Insurance, Loan Protection, Credit Life, and Term Plan products.

<USER_REQUEST>
Update the "New" stage interaction flow in the Insurance CRM Lead Detail Page.

The current design incorrectly allows the "Request Callback" button to move the lead to the next stage. This is not aligned with the insurance sales process.

The CRM should follow a strict state-machine approach where stage progression is controlled by meaningful customer interactions, not call outcomes.

---

## BUSINESS RULE

The "New" stage represents:

"We have not yet had a successful conversation with the customer."

A lead should remain in the New bucket until an IBM agent successfully speaks with the customer.

Only one action should move a lead from New → Contacted:

✓ Connected

All other outcomes should remain inside New and create follow-up actions.

---

## REMOVE CURRENT FLOW

Remove:

* Request Callback as a primary action
* Any logic where callback moves the lead to Contacted

The following behavior should no longer exist:

Request Callback
→ Contacted

This is incorrect.

---

Keep the customer contact card.

Show:

Customer Name
Mobile Number
Copy Number
Recommended Product
Loan Amount
Linked Home Loan Context

---

## PRIMARY ACTIONS

Replace current actions with only two primary options:

[ Connected ]
[ Not Connected ]

Connected = Positive outcome

Not Connected = Unsuccessful attempt

When agent clicks:

✓ Connected

Open a lightweight confirmation modal:

Conversation completed?

[ Move to Contacted ]
[ Cancel ]

Lead moved to Contacted

## FUNNEL INTEGRITY RULE

The Contacted bucket should only contain leads where a real conversation happened.

Do NOT move leads to Contacted because:

* Callback Requested
* Busy
* Switched Off
* Not Reachable
* Voicemail
* Ringing No Answer

These are outreach attempts, not successful customer engagement.

## STATE MACHINE

NEW

├── Connected
│
└── Move to CONTACTED

NEW

├── Customer Busy
├── Not Reachable
├── Switched Off
├── Callback Requested
├── Ringing No Answer
├── Voicemail
├── Customer Disconnected Call
└── Invalid Number

(All remain in NEW)

## REPORTING IMPACT

Dashboard metrics should now be accurate:

New Leads =
Leads where successful conversation has not happened.

Contacted Leads =
Leads where agent successfully connected and engaged with customer.

This change ensures funnel reporting, conversion calculations, and follow-up tracking remain accurate and operationally meaningful.

│
│    Action:
│    Remain In Contacted
│
└── Not Interested
↓
Move To Lost

---

## REPORTING LOGIC

Contacted Count

Should only include:

Leads where conversation happened but customer has not yet committed to evaluating quotes.

Quote Count

Should include:

All leads where customer explicitly requested insurance quotations.

This ensures accurate conversion reporting:

New
→ Contacted
→ Quote
→ Processing
→ Policy

and eliminates ambiguity caused by "Interested - Need Quote" remaining inside Contacted.

---

## UI CHANGES

Replace buttons:

Current:

[ Interested ]
[ Think Later ]

New:

[ Interested ]
[ Follow-up Required ]

Below:

[ Not Interested ]

with loss reason dropdown.

Interested = Move To Quote

Follow-up Required = Stay In Contacted

Not Interested = Move To Lost

This should be enforced through the CRM state machine and not left to manual stage updates by agents.

<USER_REQUEST>
Use this as a product/design prompt for the Quote + PolicyBazaar workspace implementation.

---

# Insurance CRM – Quote Stage & PolicyBazaar Workspace

## Objective

Design the Quote stage of the Insurance CRM such that IBM agents can generate quotes, share quotes, generate payment links, collect payment confirmation, and move leads to Processing without leaving Sangam.

The goal is to make the workflow extremely simple and action-oriented, similar to how the New and Contacted stages work today.

Agents should never wonder:

* What should I do next?
* What is pending?
* Why is the lead stuck?
* What status should I select?

The system should always guide the next action.

---

# Stage Flow

```text
New
↓
Contacted
↓
Quote
↓
Processing
↓
Policy
↓
Lost
```

Quote stage begins only when:

```text
Contacted
Status = Interested
Sub Status = Need Quote
```

System automatically moves lead into Quote stage.

---

# Quote Stage Philosophy

Do NOT create micro-level stages.

Things like:

* Quote generated
* Quote shared via WhatsApp
* Payment link generated
* Payment proof uploaded

should be Activity Timeline events.

The Quote stage should only represent where the customer stands in the buying journey.

---

# Quote Stage Layout

Follow existing Sangam layout.

---

## Left Panel

Application Data Checklist

Show completion status:

### Insurance Details

* Product Selected
* Insurer Selected
* Plan Selected

### Customer Details

* Name
* DOB
* Mobile
* Email
* Address

### Loan Details

* Loan Amount
* Bank Name
* HL Stage

### Nominee Details

* Name
* Relationship
* DOB

### Health Declaration

* Smoker
* Existing Illness
* Existing Policies

Legend:

```text
Green = Complete
Orange = Pending
Grey = Missing
```

---

## Center Panel

Stage Tracker

```text
New
Contacted
Quote
Processing
Policy
Lost
```

Quote highlighted.

---

# Quote Workspace

Main content area.

---

## Section 1

Recommended Product

Example:

```text
Recommended Product

Loan Protection

Reason:
₹45L home loan
Ag
<truncated 3034 bytes>
ter generation.

Show:

```text
Share via WhatsApp
```

```text
Share via Email
```

```text
Copy Payment Link
```

Activity Log:

```text
Payment link generated
```

```text
Payment link shared via WhatsApp
```

---

# Payment Proof Section

Inside Quote stage.

Card:

```text
Payment Confirmation
```

Fields:

### Upload Screenshot

### Upload Receipt

### Enter UTR

### Remarks

---

# Verification Status

Display:

```text
Payment Verification

Pending
Verified
Rejected
```

---

# Verification Outcomes

### Pending

Lead remains in Quote.

---

### Rejected

Status options:

* Invalid Payment Proof
* Amount Mismatch
* Wrong Transaction

Lead remains in Quote.

---

### Verified

System:

```text
Status = Payment Verified
```

Automatically:

```text
Move lead to Processing
```

Activity:

```text
Payment verified

Lead moved to Processing
```

---

# Quote Stage Lost Flow

Agent can directly mark Lost.

Reasons:

### Quote Declined

### Premium Too High

### Existing Insurance

### Purchased Elsewhere

### Customer Not Interested

### No Response After Quote

### Deal Postponed

### Payment Not Received

System:

```text
Quote
→
Lost
```

---

# Next Action Widget

Always visible on right side.

Examples:

### Quote not shared

```text
Next Action:
Generate Quote
```

### Quote shared

```text
Next Action:
Follow up on customer decision
```

### Plan selected

```text
Next Action:
Generate Payment Link
```

### Payment link shared

```text
Next Action:
Verify payment
```

This widget should drive agent behavior exactly like New and Contacted stages do.

---

# Success Criteria

An IBM agent should be able to:

1. Generate quote.
2. Compare plans.
3. Share quote.
4. Track customer decision.
5. Generate payment link.
6. Collect payment proof.
7. Verify payment.
8. Move lead to Processing.

Without leaving Sangam and without needing more than 1–2 status updates during the entire Quote journey.

Absolutely. Below is the version I would actually put in the PRD because it explains:

1. What the bucket means
2. What statuses are available
3. What sub-statuses are available
4. When the bucket changes
5. What action the agent should take

---

# Insurance CRM State Machine

## Bucket 1: NEW

### Purpose

Customer has not yet been successfully engaged regarding insurance.

The agent is attempting first contact.

---

## Status: Not Connected

### Sub Status

* Customer Busy
* Not Reachable
* Switched Off
* Ringing No Answer
* Voicemail
* Invalid Number
* Customer Disconnected Call

### Agent Action

Schedule follow-up and retry.

### Bucket Movement

Remain in:

```text
NEW
```

---

## Trigger to Move Bucket

When agent successfully speaks with customer and updates:

```text
Status = Callback
OR
Status = Interested
OR
Status = Not Interested
```

System automatically moves lead to:

```text
CONTACTED
```

---

# Bucket 2: CONTACTED

### Purpose

Customer has been contacted and insurance discussion has happened.

Agent is now qualifying interest.

---

## Status: Callback

### Sub Status

* Busy Call Later
* Discussing With Family
* Need More Information
* Comparing Options
* Language Barrier
* Waiting For Decision

### Agent Action

Follow up later.

### Bucket Movement

Remain in:

```text
CONTACTED
```

---

## Status: Interested

### Sub Status

* Need Quote
* Need Product Comparison
* Need Benefit Illustration
* Need Premium Clarification

### Agent Action

Generate and share insurance quote.

### Bucket Movement

Remain in:

```text
CONTACTED
```

until quote is generated.

---

## Trigger to Move Bucket

When agent shares quote with customer.

System automatically updates:

```text
Status = Quote Shared
```

and moves lead to:

```text
QUOTE
```

---

## Status: Not Interested

### Sub Status

* Already Insured
* Too Expensive
* Coverage Not Needed
* Purchased Elsewhere
* Bank Insurance Selected

### Bucket Movement

```text
LOST
```

---

# Bucket 3: QUOTE

### Purpose

Customer is evalu
<truncated 2455 bytes>
et 5: POLICY

### Purpose

Policy has been issued successfully.

Now post-issuance operations are tracked.

---

## Status: Active

### Sub Status

* Policy Shared
* Free Look Active
* MIS Updated
* Commission Pending

### Agent Action

Monitor post-policy activities.

### Bucket Movement

Remain in:

```text
POLICY
```

---

## Status: Completed

### Sub Status

* Commission Released

### Agent Action

No further action required.

### Bucket Movement

Remain in:

```text
POLICY
```

---

## Status: Cancelled

### Sub Status

* Free Look Cancellation
* Customer Cancellation

### Bucket Movement

```text
LOST
```

---

# Bucket 6: LOST

### Purpose

Lead can no longer be converted.

---

## Lost Categories

### Not Interested

* Already Insured
* Too Expensive
* Coverage Not Needed
* Purchased Elsewhere

---

### Insurer Rejected

* Medical
* Financial
* Risk

---

### Policy Cancelled

* Free Look
* Customer Request

---

# Final Backend Mapping

| Status              | Bucket     |
| ------------------- | ---------- |
| Not Connected       | New        |
| Callback            | Contacted  |
| Interested          | Contacted  |
| Quote Shared        | Quote      |
| Payment Link Shared | Quote      |
| Payment Verified    | Processing |
| In Progress         | Processing |
| Counter Offer       | Processing |
| Policy Issued       | Policy     |
| Active              | Policy     |
| Completed           | Policy     |
| Not Interested      | Lost       |
| Insurer Rejected    | Lost       |
| Cancelled           | Lost       |

### Simplified Funnel

```text
NEW
↓
CONTACTED
↓
QUOTE
↓
PROCESSING
↓
POLICY

Any negative outcome
↓
LOST
```

One refinement I'd make before handover: **do not let agents manually select the bucket**. Let them only select Status + Sub Status, and let the backend derive the bucket automatically. This will keep your reporting clean and prevent accidental stage jumps.

# NEW Bucket

### Purpose

Agent has not yet qualified the lead.

## Not Connected

* Customer Busy
* Not Reachable
* Switched Off
* Ringing No Answer

* Need Coverage Clarification

* Coverage Not Needed

# What I Would Actually Implement

If I were building Sangam, I'd make it even cleaner:

### NEW

```text
Not Connected
Callback
Interested
Not Interested
```

### CONTACTED

```text
Callback
Interested
Not Interested
```

### QUOTE

```text
Quote Shared
Payment Link Shared
Payment Done
Not Interested
```

### PROCESSING

```text
In Progress
Counter Offer
Insurer Rejected
Policy Issued
```

### POLICY

```text
Active
Completed
Cancelled
```

This gives agents only **13 top-level statuses across the entire CRM**, which is easy to learn and report on, while the sub-statuses provide the detail needed for operations and analytics.

<USER_REQUEST>
Build a complete Insurance CRM State Machine inside Sangam CRM.

The system should be designed so that agents never manually change buckets/stages.

Agents only update:

1. Status
2. Sub Status
3. Remarks
4. Follow-up Date (when applicable)

The backend automatically determines and updates the bucket.

---

BUCKETS

---

The CRM has 6 buckets:

1. New
2. Contacted
3. Quote
4. Processing
5. Policy
6. Lost

Buckets should be shown as the stage tracker on the lead detail page.

Agents cannot manually edit buckets.

Buckets are derived from status changes.

---

STATE MACHINE PRINCIPLE

---

Agent updates:

Status
Sub Status

System updates:

Bucket

Activity Timeline

Lead History

Follow-up Tasks

ACTIVITY TIMELINE

---

Every status update should automatically create timeline entries.

Examples:

Quote Shared

Policy Cancelled

Agent Name

Old Status

New Status

Remarks

---

---

Allow managers to see:

Status progression

Bucket progression

Agent actions

Timestamps

FOLLOW-UP TASK ENGINE

---

Not Connected
Callback

Require:

Follow-up Date
Follow-up Time

Display in:

Manager Dashboard

VALIDATION RULES

---

Do not allow:

Quote generation without mandatory customer details.

Payment verification without proof upload.

Policy Issued without policy document upload.

Counter Offer Accepted without remarks.

---

SUCCESS CRITERIA

---

Agents should only think:

"What happened with the customer?"

The system should automatically determine:

Bucket

Timeline

Follow-up

Reporting

State transitions

without requiring agents to manually move leads between stages.

<USER_REQUEST>
Prompt: Simplify Quote Bucket for V1
Objective

Redesign the Quote bucket to be operationally simple.

The CRM should not attempt to recreate insurer journeys inside the application.

Instead:

CRM provides access to quote generation tools.
CRM tracks lead progression through statuses.
CRM stores proof and audit logs.
Actual quote generation and payment flows continue to happen through insurer systems and PolicyBazaar.
Design Principles
Remove Journey Tracker

Remove:

Generate
Select
Share
Link
Send Link
Proof
Verified

This creates unnecessary complexity.

The status engine already tracks progression.

Showing both creates duplicate workflows.

Quote Bucket Layout

The center section should contain only:

Product Selection

Tabs:

Loan Protection
Property Insurance
Credit Life
Term Plan

Agent can switch between products until payment is verified.

Display:

Selected Product:
Term Plan

Change Product
Loan Protection

Display:

In-House Quote Calculator

Show:

CARE Health
Premium: ₹14,500

[Select Plan]
TATA AIG
Premium: ₹16,200

[Select Plan]

After selection:

Selected Plan:
CARE Health

Premium:
₹14,500

No further UI.

No payment link UI.

No quote share UI.

No journey tracker.

Property Insurance

Display:

Property Insurance Calculator

Show plans.

Agent selects plan.

Display:

Selected Plan:
Bajaj General

Premium:
₹1,276

Nothing else.

Credit Life

Display:

Open PolicyBazaar Workspace
Customer details are prefilled.

[Open PolicyBazaar]

Opening launches iframe drawer.

No additional CRM workflow.

Term Plan

Display:

Open PolicyBazaar Workspace
Customer details are prefilled.

[Open PolicyBazaar]

Opening launches iframe drawer.

No additional CRM workflow.

PolicyBazaar Drawer

When agent clicks:

Open PolicyBazaar

Open right-side drawer.

Width: 70–80%.

Inside drawer:

Embedded PB iframe.

What Happens Inside PB

Agent:

fills details
compares plans
generates quote
discusses with customer
reaches payment page

All inside PB.

CRM should not duplicate these steps.

Add Single Utility Action

At bottom of iframe:

Copy Payment Link

Behavior:

Copies current PB payment URL.

Agent can then:

send WhatsApp manually
send Email manually

Do NOT build:

WhatsApp integration
Email integration
Quote sharing module

for V1.

Status Updates Drive Workflow

CRM progression happens from right panel.

Not from center workspace.

Quote Bucket Statuses

enabled.

allowed.

Product

<USER_REQUEST>
Yes, I went through the PRD you shared in detail. 

And after comparing it with all our discussions over the last few days, I think the PRD is currently trying to do **too much** and is mixing three different things:

1. CRM Workflow
2. Insurance Operations Workflow
3. Insurer/PolicyBazaar Workflow

These should be separated.

---

# What I Would Change in the PRD

## 1. Simplify the Buckets

Current PRD:

```text
New
Contacted
Quote
Payment
Processing
Policy
Closed
Lost
```

What we finalized:

```text
New
Contacted
Quote
Processing
Policy
Lost
```

Remove:

```text
Payment
Closed
```

Reason:

Payment is not a stage.

Payment is an outcome within Quote.

Similarly, Closed is not needed.

Policy is effectively the terminal success state.

---

# 2. Simplify State Machine

Current PRD has too many micro-statuses.

Example:

```text
Need Product Comparison
Need Premium Clarification
Need Coverage Clarification
Need More Information
Discussing With Family
Comparing Options
```

These are CRM notes.

Not statuses.

---

Instead:

# NEW

Visible Statuses

```text
Not Connected
Call Back
Interested
Not Interested
```

Sub Statuses

### Not Connected

```text
Customer Busy
Not Reachable
Invalid Number
Ringing No Answer
Switched Off
Voicemail
Customer Disconnected
```

### Call Back

```text
Busy Call Later
Call Later - Partial Details Shared
Language Barrier
Customer Disconnected
```

### Interested

No sub-status

### Not Interested

```text
Already Insured
Too Expensive
Coverage Not Needed
Purchased Elsewhere
Bank Insurance Selected
```

---

Transition Rules

```text
Call Back
→ Contacted

Interested
→ Contacted

Not Interested
→ Lost

Not Connected
→ Remains New
```

---

# CONTACTED

Visible Statuses

```text
Call Back
Interested
Not Interested
```

---

Call Back

```text
Busy Call Later
Need More Time
Discussing With Family
```

---

Interested

No sub-status

---

Not Interested

```text
Already Insured
Too Expensive
Purchased Elsewhere
Coverage Not Needed
```

---

Transition

```text
Ge
<truncated 1913 bytes>
``text
CARE Quote Card

TATA Quote Card

Select Plan
```

That's all.

No payment link.

No quote tracking.

No share tracking.

No journey tracker.

---

### Property / Credit Life / Term

Show:

```text
Open PolicyBazaar Workspace
```

Button.

Click.

Open iframe drawer.

---

Inside PB:

```text
Compare Plans
Generate Quote
Share Quote
Generate Payment Link
```

Everything happens there.

---

CRM does not duplicate PB workflow.

---

When PB reaches final payment screen:

Show:

```text
Copy Payment Link
```

Button.

Agent manually shares via WhatsApp.

---

No WhatsApp button.

No Email button.

No CRM integration.

---

# Payment Verification

Current PRD says:

```text
Upload Payment Proof Optional
```

I disagree.

For Ambak process:

Make it mandatory.

---

When:

```text
Status = Payment Done
Sub Status = Payment Verified
```

Show:

```text
Upload Payment Proof *
```

Required.

Without proof:

```text
Update Status Disabled
```

---

# Activity History

Current PRD is missing operational logs.

Need logs like:

```text
Status updated to Interested

Lead moved to Contacted

Plan Selected: CARE Health

PolicyBazaar Workspace Opened

Payment Link Shared

Payment Proof Uploaded

Lead moved to Processing
```

---

# Final Recommendation

If I were rewriting this PRD for Engineering, I would keep only these modules:

1. Executive Summary
2. Lead Creation
3. Lead Detail Page Layout
4. State Machine
5. Quote Management
6. Processing Workflow
7. Policy Workflow
8. Activity History
9. API & Data Model
10. Permissions

And completely remove:

* Journey tracker
* Payment stage
* Closed stage
* Deep quote workflow tracking
* CRM-side WhatsApp sharing
* CRM-side email sharing
* Micro statuses like Need Premium Clarification, Need Product Comparison, etc.

That will reduce the PRD by almost 40% while making it much closer to how IBM agents actually work today and much easier for engineering to build.

<USER_REQUEST>
Update the Insurance Lead Creation workflow to match the PRD.

Current behavior:
When no Home Loan lead is found, the system shows a "No home loan lead found" error state with a "Create Fresh Lead" CTA.

Replace this flow completely.

New behavior:

1. User searches by Mobile Number or HL Lead ID.

2. If HL Lead is found:
   - Pre-fill customer and loan information.
   - Continue existing flow.

3. If HL Lead is NOT found:
   - Immediately show a Manual Insurance Lead Creation form.
   - Do NOT show an error state.
   - Do NOT show "Create Fresh Lead".

Form Fields:

Customer Details
- First Name (required)
- Last Name (required)
- Mobile Number (required)
- Email ID (optional)
- DOB (optional)
- Gender (optional)

Insurance Details
- Insurance Product (required)
  - Loan Protection
  - Property Insurance
  - Credit Life
  - Term Plan

- Lead Source (required)
  - Manual
  - D2C
  - Sangam
  - Saathi
  - Yoddha

- Assigned IBM Agent (required)

Optional Loan Details
- Lender
- Loan Amount
- Loan Stage

CTA:
"Create Insurance Lead"

On submit:
- Create insurance lead
- Bucket = New
- Status = Null
- Source = Manual
- Redirect to Lead Detail Page

Also remove all UI where agents manually move buckets.

The system should only allow status updates.

Backend state machine must automatically decide bucket transitions based on status selection.

Remove buttons like:
- Move to Contacted
- Move to Quote
- Move to Processing

Agents update Status.
Backend updates Bucket.
</USER_REQUEST>

<USER_REQUEST>
Here's my thinking on the center panel experience for each stage, and exactly what the right panel should show at each point:

NEW — "Just call them"
Center panel is deliberately empty of insurance content. The lead just arrived. The agent's only job is to call the customer. So:

Center panel: Activity History tabs pushed up to fill the space (Activity History, Follow Up, Documents — same tabs that exist in Sangam HL CRM). No insurance-specific content yet. The agent calls, records the outcome via the right panel, and moves on.
Right panel: Status dropdown shows New bucket options (Not Connected / Call Back / Interested / Not Interested). Follow-up date picker when Call Back is selected. Remarks. Save.

This is the simplest stage. No clutter.

CONTACTED — "Understand what they need"
The agent has spoken to the customer. Now they need to understand which insurance product fits. Center panel becomes an education + selection tool:

Center panel: Four product cards in a 2×2 grid. Each card shows the product name, a 2-line description, key benefit, and which insurers are available. Agent taps a product to select it — the card highlights. Below the grid: "Generate Quote →" button (disabled until a product is selected). Clicking this moves the lead to the Quote bucket with the selected product recorded.
Right panel: Status dropdown (Call Back / Interested / Not Interested). Same as before. The "Generate Quote" action is in the center panel — it's a deliberate action, not a status update.


QUOTE — "Generate and share the quote"
This is where the product-specific experience kicks in. Two paths:
Path A — Loan Protection (CARE + TATA):

Center panel shows the in-house calculator. Agent inputs age, loan amount, tenure, plan type. Hits calculate. Gets CARE and TATA cards with premiums. Selects a plan. That's it. No payment link from CRM — insurer sends it directly.
Path B — Property / Credit Life / Term (PolicyBazaar):

Center panel shows a "Open PolicyBazaar Workspace" launch card. Clicki
<truncated 647 bytes>
tically.

PROCESSING — "Track insurer milestones"
This is where the milestone tracker lives. The center panel shows a vertical milestone tracker that is product-specific. Each product has its own set of milestones:
Property Insurance (4 milestones):

Payment Verified ✓ (already done)
KYC Documents (Aadhaar + PAN)
Policy Issued
Policy Copy Received

LP — CARE (5 milestones):

Payment Verified ✓
Verification (CARE verifies)
Feder Form (customer declaration)
Policy Issued
Policy Copy Received

LP — TATA AIG (5 milestones):

Payment Verified ✓
Tele-PD Scheduled
Tele-PD Completed
Policy Issued
Policy Copy Received

Credit Life (7 milestones):

Payment Verified ✓
KYC Verification
Income Verification
Medical Examination
Underwriting Review
Approval Decision
Policy Issued

Term Plan (7 milestones):

Same as Credit Life.
The milestone tracker shows: Done (green, collapsed, shows date), Active (expanded with what's needed), Pending (gray, collapsed). Only one milestone is active at a time.
Right panel: Status dropdown shows Processing bucket options (Documents / Medical / Approval / Policy Issuance). Sub-status options change per status. Agent updates status as milestones complete. On "Policy Issuance: Issued" → lead moves to Policy.
The milestone tracker in the center panel is a read-only visual that reflects the status updates made via the right panel. The agent does not interact with the milestones directly — they update the status on the right, and the milestone tracker advances automatically.

POLICY — "Close it out"
Center panel shows the policy summary form:

Policy Number (agent enters)
Policy Start Date (agent enters)
Insurer (auto-populated from payment verification)
Premium Paid (auto-populated)
Freelook Expiry (system-calculated)
Commission Expected (20% of premium, indicative)

Right panel: Status dropdown shows Policy bucket options (Active / Freelook / Payout). Standard flow.
</USER_REQUEST>

<USER_REQUEST>
please re think on this on my prompt 


Here's my thinking on the center panel experience for each stage, and exactly what the right panel should show at each point:

NEW — "Just call them"
Center panel is deliberately empty of insurance content. The lead just arrived. The agent's only job is to call the customer. So:

Center panel: Activity History tabs pushed up to fill the space (Activity History, Follow Up, Documents — same tabs that exist in Sangam HL CRM). No insurance-specific content yet. The agent calls, records the outcome via the right panel, and moves on.
Right panel: Status dropdown shows New bucket options (Not Connected / Call Back / Interested / Not Interested). Follow-up date picker when Call Back is selected. Remarks. Save.

This is the simplest stage. No clutter.

CONTACTED — "Understand what they need"
The agent has spoken to the customer. Now they need to understand which insurance product fits. Center panel becomes an education + selection tool:

Center panel: Four product cards in a 2×2 grid. Each card shows the product name, a 2-line description, key benefit, and which insurers are available. Agent taps a product to select it — the card highlights. Below the grid: "Generate Quote →" button (disabled until a product is selected). Clicking this moves the lead to the Quote bucket with the selected product recorded.
Right panel: Status dropdown (Call Back / Interested / Not Interested). Same as before. The "Generate Quote" action is in the center panel — it's a deliberate action, not a status update.


QUOTE — "Generate and share the quote"
This is where the product-specific experience kicks in. Two paths:
Path A — Loan Protection (CARE + TATA):

Center panel shows the in-house calculator. Agent inputs age, loan amount, tenure, plan type. Hits calculate. Gets CARE and TATA cards with premiums. Selects a plan. That's it. No payment link from CRM — insurer sends it directly.
Path B — Property / Credit Life / Term (PolicyBazaar):

Center panel shows a "Open Pol
<truncated 998 bytes>
 + PAN)
Policy Issued
Policy Copy Received

LP — CARE (5 milestones):

Payment Verified ✓
Verification (CARE verifies)
Feder Form (customer declaration)
Policy Issued
Policy Copy Received

LP — TATA AIG (5 milestones):

Payment Verified ✓
Tele-PD Scheduled
Tele-PD Completed
Policy Issued
Policy Copy Received

Credit Life (7 milestones):

Payment Verified ✓
KYC Verification
Income Verification
Medical Examination
Underwriting Review
Approval Decision
Policy Issued

Term Plan (7 milestones):

Same as Credit Life.
The milestone tracker shows: Done (green, collapsed, shows date), Active (expanded with what's needed), Pending (gray, collapsed). Only one milestone is active at a time.
Right panel: Status dropdown shows Processing bucket options (Documents / Medical / Approval / Policy Issuance). Sub-status options change per status. Agent updates status as milestones complete. On "Policy Issuance: Issued" → lead moves to Policy.
The milestone tracker in the center panel is a read-only visual that reflects the status updates made via the right panel. The agent does not interact with the milestones directly — they update the status on the right, and the milestone tracker advances automatically.

POLICY — "Close it out"
Center panel shows the policy summary form:

Policy Number (agent enters)
Policy Start Date (agent enters)
Insurer (auto-populated from payment verification)
Premium Paid (auto-populated)
Freelook Expiry (system-calculated)
Commission Expected (20% of premium, indicative)

Right panel: Status dropdown shows Policy bucket options (Active / Freelook / Payout). Standard flow.

<USER_REQUEST>
I think removing the **Action column** is absolutely the right decision.

The moment agents start working at scale (100-300 leads), they stop using buttons inside tables and start using:

* Filters
* Sorting
* Follow-up queues
* Status queues
* Click row → open lead

The Action button is consuming valuable horizontal space that can be used for more meaningful information.

---

# 1. Remove Action Column

Current:

```text
Insurance ID
Customer
Product & Source
Loan Amount
Stage
Status
Status Update
IBM Agent
Action
```

Proposed:

```text
Insurance ID
Customer
Product
Loan
Stage
Status
Follow-up
Last Activity
IBM Agent
```

Clicking anywhere on the row opens Lead Detail.

---

# 2. Most Important Filter Missing

For an IBM Agent, the biggest question is:

> "Which customer should I call next?"

Not:

> "Which lead belongs to Tata?"

---

## Follow-Up Filter

```text
All
Follow-up Due Today
Overdue Follow-up
Upcoming Follow-up
No Follow-up Scheduled
```

This will become the most used filter.

---

# 3. My Recommendation for Filters

### Primary Filters

```text
Stage
Product
Source
```

Keep.

---

### Add Status Filter

```text
All

Not Connected
Call Back
Interested
Not Interested

Quote Shared
Payment Link Shared
Payment Done

Documents
Medical
Approval

Policy Active
Freelook
Payout
```

Very useful.

---

### Add Insurer Filter

```text
All

CARE
TATA AIG

Policy Bazaar

ICICI
HDFC
Bajaj
SBI
```

Agents often work insurer-wise.

---

### Add Follow-up Filter

```text
Overdue
Today
Tomorrow
This Week
No Follow-up
```

---

### Add Assignment Filter

```text
Assigned to Me
Unassigned
```

---

### Add Loan Amount Filter

```text
0-20L
20-40L
40-60L
60L+
```

High value customers first.

---

### Add Payment Filter

```text
Payment Pending
Payment Verified
Verification Failed
```

---

# 4. Sorting Options

Current CRM has none.

I would add:

### Sort By

```text
Newest First
Oldest First

Recently Updated

Highest Loan Amount
Lowest Loan Amount

Follow-up Date

Recently Assigned

Longest Pend
<truncated 473 bytes>
43210
Age 32
```

---

# 7. Loan Column Can Be Richer

Current:

```text
₹45L
HDFC Bank
```

I would show:

```text
₹45L
HDFC Bank
Login Done
```

or

```text
₹45L
HDFC Bank
Sanctioned
```

Because insurance conversion probability depends heavily on HL stage.

---

# 8. Add Lead Age Column

Extremely important.

```text
Created 2 hrs ago
Created 3 days ago
Created 12 days ago
```

or

```text
Lead Age
```

Example:

```text
2 Days
7 Days
15 Days
```

Managers love this.

---

# 9. Add Priority Column

Auto-generated.

Example:

```text
🔥 Hot

🟡 Warm

⚪ Cold
```

Logic:

```text
Interested + Follow-up Today
= Hot

Quote Shared
= Hot

Payment Pending
= Hot

Not Connected
= Warm

No Activity 15 Days
= Cold
```

This becomes an excellent queue management system.

---

# 10. Recommended Final Table

Instead of:

```text
Insurance ID
Customer Details
Product & Source
Loan Amount
Stage
Status
Status Update
IBM Agent
Action
```

I would do:

```text
Insurance ID

Customer
(Name + Mobile + Age)

Product
(Product + Insurer)

Loan
(Amount + Bank + HL Stage)

Stage

Status

Next Follow-up

Lead Age

Priority

IBM Agent
```

---

# Even Better (V2)

If you want this CRM to feel like a proper sales CRM, add these two columns:

```text
Last Call Outcome
```

Example:

```text
Busy
Need Quote
Call Tomorrow
```

and

```text
Last Activity
```

Example:

```text
Status Updated
2 hrs ago

Quote Shared
Yesterday

Payment Verified
5 mins ago
```

---

If I were optimizing purely for IBM agent productivity, my final columns would be:

```text
Insurance ID
Customer
Product
Loan
Stage
Status
Next Follow-up
Lead Age
Priority
Last Activity
```

and completely remove:

```text
Action
IBM Agent (for agent view)
```

Keep IBM Agent column only for Manager view.

This will make the table much more operational and help agents decide **who to call next**, which is ultimately the primary job-to-be-done of this screen.

These are filters agents use every day.

```text

[ Status ▼ ]
[ Search Lead ]
[ More Filters ]

Clicking:

```text

opens a modal like the screenshot you shared.

# One Additional Filter I Strongly Recommend

### Pending With

This will become one of the most useful filters for managers.

```text
Customer

IBM Agent

PolicyBazaar

CARE

TATA

Insurer

Operations Team
```

Example:

```text
Show all cases pending with customer
```

or

```text
Show all cases pending with insurer
```

This filter will help managers instantly identify bottlenecks without opening individual leads.

---

### UX Recommendation

Use a **right-side slide-over drawer** (similar to the screenshot) instead of a small dropdown popover.

Reason:

* Supports 15–20 filters comfortably.
* Easier to add future filters.
* Works well on laptops.
* Feels consistent with enterprise CRMs like Salesforce, HubSpot, Freshsales, and Ambak's existing internal tools.

For your insurance CRM, I would keep only **4 filters visible by default**:

```text
Stage
Product
Source
Status
```

Everything else should live inside the **More Filters drawer**. This keeps the dashboard clean while still allowing power users to drill down deeply when needed.

<USER_REQUEST>
# Insurance CRM – Lead State Machine v1.0

## Objective

The purpose of the state machine is to provide a standardized workflow for all insurance leads irrespective of product type (Loan Protection, Property Insurance, Credit Life, Term Plan).

The CRM should display only the primary buckets to agents:

1. New
2. Contacted
3. Quote
4. Payment Done
5. Policy

The bucket movement will happen automatically in the backend based on status updates selected by the IBM Agent.

---

# 1. NEW BUCKET

## Purpose

Lead has been created but meaningful discussion with customer has not happened yet.

---

## Status: Not Connected

### Sub Statuses

* Customer Busy
* Not Reachable
* Switched Off
* Ringing No Answer
* Voicemail
* Customer Disconnected Call

### UI Behaviour

Show:

* Follow-up Date (Mandatory)
* Pending With = Customer

### Bucket Movement

Remains in New bucket.

---

## Status: Call Back

### Bucket Movement

| Quote          | Payment Done - Verified | Payment Done        |
| Payment Done   | Policy Copy Issued      | Policy              |
| Any Bucket     | Lost Reason Selected    | Lost (Hidden State) |

# Insurance CRM – Lead State Machine v1.0

## Objective

The purpose of the state machine is to provide a standardized workflow for all insurance leads irrespective of product type (Loan Protection, Property Insurance, Credit Life, Term Plan).

The CRM should display only the primary buckets to agents:

1. New
2. Contacted
3. Quote
4. Payment Done
5. Policy

The bucket movement will happen automatically in the backend based on status updates selected by the IBM Agent.

---

# 1. NEW BUCKET

## Purpose

Lead has been created but meaningful discussion with customer has not happened yet.

---

## Status: Not Connected

### Sub Statuses

* Customer Busy
* Not Reachable
* Switched Off
* Ringing No Answer
* Voicemail
* Customer Disconnected Call

### UI Behaviour

Show:

* Follow-up Date (Mandatory)
* Pending With = Customer

### Bucket Movement

Remains in New bucket.

---

## Status: Call Back

### Sub Statuses

* Busy, Call Later
* Call Later - Partial Discussion
* Customer Disconnected Call
* Language Barrier

### UI Behaviour

Show:

* Follow-up Date (Mandatory)
* Pending With = Customer

### Bucket Movement

Move to Contacted bucket.

---

## Status: Interested

### Sub Statuses

* Need Quote

### UI Behaviour

No follow-up mandatory.

### Bucket Movement

Move to Contacted bucket.

---

## Status: Not Interested

### Sub Statuses

* Too Expensive
* Already Insured
* Not Required
* Will Purchase Later
* Family Not Interested
* Other

### Bucket Movement

Move to Contacted bucket.

Lead remains active unless explicitly marked lost later.

| Current Bucket | Status                  | Next Bucket         |
| -------------- | ----------------------- | ------------------- |

| Payment Done   | Policy Copy Issued      | Policy              |
| Any Bucket     | Lost Reason Selected    | Lost (Hidden State) |

3.4 PAYMENT DONE
Purpose

Customer payment has been successfully received.

All fulfilment and insurer processing activities happen in this bucket.

This bucket replaces the earlier Processing stage.

Product-Specific Processing Flows
Property Insurance

Workflow:

Payment Verified
→ KYC Pending
→ KYC Completed
→ Policy Issued

Expected TAT:

Few minutes to few hours.

Loan Protection (CARE)

Workflow:

Payment Verified
→ Proposal Form Pending
→ Proposal Form Completed
→ Policy Issued

Loan Protection (TATA)

Workflow:

Payment Verified
→ Tele-PD Pending
→ Tele-PD Completed
→ Policy Issued

Credit Life

Workflow:

Payment Verified
→ Documents Pending
→ Documents Received
→ Medical Scheduled
→ Medical Completed
→ Underwriting Review
→ Counter Offer (Optional)
→ Approval
→ Policy Issued

Expected TAT:

7–10 Days

Term Plan

Workflow:

Payment Verified
→ Documents Pending
→ Documents Received
→ Medical Scheduled
→ Medical Completed
→ Underwriting Review
→ Counter Offer (Optional)
→ Approval
→ Policy Issued

Expected TAT:

7–15 Days

Processing Statuses
Documents

Sub Statuses:

Pending
Partial
Received

Applicable Products:

Credit Life
Term Plan
KYC

Sub Statuses:

Pending
Completed

Applicable Products:

Property Insurance
Proposal Form

Sub Statuses:

Pending
Completed

Applicable Products:

CARE Loan Protection
Tele-PD

Sub Statuses:

Pending
Completed

Applicable Products:

TATA Loan Protection
Medical

Sub Statuses:

Scheduled
Completed

Applicable Products:

Credit Life
Term Plan
Underwriting

Sub Statuses:

Pending
Counter Offer
Approved
Rejected

Special Rule:

If Counter Offer selected:

Capture:

Counter Offer Amount
Customer Response
Additional Premium Received
Policy Copy

Sub Statuses:

Pending
Issued

Mandatory Field:

Policy Copy Upload

Bucket Movement:

Payment Done → Policy

Condition:

Policy Copy = Issued

# Prompt: Implement Quote Creation Module Inside Insurance CRM

## Objective

Build the Quote Creation experience inside the Insurance CRM Quote Bucket.

The goal is to enable IBM agents to generate, compare, select and share insurance quotes for different insurance products from a single CRM workflow.

The Quote module should dynamically change based on the selected insurance product.

Supported products:

1. Loan Protection
2. Property Insurance
3. Credit Life
4. Term Plan

---

# Overall UI Structure

Inside the Quote Bucket, replace the generic calculator section with a dynamic product-specific quote generation workspace.

Layout:

```text
---------------------------------------------------
Application Data                     Update Status
---------------------------------------------------

NEW > CONTACTED > QUOTE > PAYMENT > POLICY

---------------------------------------------------
Quote Workspace
---------------------------------------------------

[Product Header]

[Product Specific Inputs]

[Generate Quote]

---------------------------------------------------

[Generated Quote Results]

Plan Card 1
Plan Card 2
Plan Card 3

---------------------------------------------------

[Activity History]
```

Only show the quote workflow relevant to the selected product.

---

# Product Selection Logic

The recommended insurance product is already available at lead level.

Examples:

```text
Loan Protection
Property Insurance
Credit Life
Term Plan
```

The quote workspace should automatically render the relevant form based on the selected product.

No page refresh.

No route change.

Dynamic component rendering only.

---

# PRODUCT 1: LOAN PROTECTION

## Display Header

```text
Loan Protection
Path A - In-house Calculator
```

---

## Input Fields

### Date of Birth

Type:

```text
Date Picker
```

Mandatory

---

### Plan Type

Type:

```text
Dr
<truncated 3777 bytes>
s

Agent generates payment link.

Update:

```text
Status:
Payment Link Shared

Sub Status:
Awaiting Payment
```

Mandatory:

```text
Follow Up Date
Pending With = Customer
```

---

## If Link Problem

Status:

```text
Payment Link Shared
```

Sub Status:

```text
Link Not Working
```

or

```text
Resend Requested
```

Mandatory:

```text
Follow Up Date
Pending With = IBM Agent
```

---

## If Customer Pays

Agent updates:

```text
Status:
Payment Done

Sub Status:
Verified
```

---

# Payment Proof Upload

When status selected:

```text
Payment Done
```

Sub Status:

```text
Verified
```

Display mandatory upload component.

Accepted:

```text
Image
PDF
Screenshot
UTR Receipt
```

Fields:

```text
Payment Amount

UTR Number

Payment Date

Proof Upload
```

Mandatory before save.

---

# Bucket Movement Rules

```text
Quote Bucket
```

remains unchanged for:

```text
Quote Shared
Payment Link Shared
Verification Pending
Verification Failed
```

Move to:

```text
Payment Done Bucket
```

only when:

```text
Status = Payment Done
Sub Status = Verified
```

---

# Activity Logging

Every action must create timeline entries.

Examples:

```text
Quote Generated
```

```text
CARE Insurance Plan Selected
```

```text
Payment Link Copied
```

```text
Payment Proof Uploaded
```

```text
Status changed from Quote Shared → Payment Link Shared
```

Store:

```text
Timestamp
Agent Name
Remarks
Source
```

---

# Design Principles

* Keep quote generation extremely simple.
* No unnecessary workflows.
* Product-specific forms only.
* PolicyBazaar handles quote generation for Credit Life and Term Plan.
* CRM only handles status tracking and workflow management.
* Minimize clicks for IBM agents.
* Every quote should be generated within 30 seconds.
* Every status update should require maximum 2 clicks.

This should be treated as the implementation specification for the Quote Bucket experience in the Insurance CRM.

Prompt to Implement

Add a global "Mark as Lost" action button in the Insurance CRM lead detail page, positioned at the top-right of the stage progress bar similar to Sangam CRM. Lost should not be a visible bucket in the stage pipeline. Clicking the button should open a modal containing:

Lost Category (dropdown)
Lost Reason (dependent dropdown)
Remarks (mandatory textarea)
Optional "Allow Re-open" checkbox

Available categories and reasons:

Customer Related

Not Interested
Already Insured
Wrong Number
Duplicate Lead
Language Barrier

Quote Related

Premium Too High
Competitor Chosen
No Response

Payment Related

Payment Not Received
Payment Failed

Underwriting Related

Medical Rejected
Counter Offer Rejected
Insurer Rejected

On save:

Lead state becomes Lost
Existing bucket history remains unchanged
Lost metadata is stored (category, reason, remarks, timestamp, agent)
Create activity log entry
Remove lead from active pipeline counts
Include lead in Lost reporting

Display a red Lost banner on the lead details page showing reason, date and agent who marked it lost. Allow authorized users to reopen the lead later and restore it to its last active bucket.

This approach keeps the stage machine clean while giving you robust loss analytics and reporting.

<USER_REQUEST>
Prompt: Redesign Insurance Lead Detail Page Around Agent Workflow
Objective

Improve the Insurance Lead Detail Page to make it easier for IBM Agents to manage leads without changing the underlying state machine.

The redesign should focus on:

Reducing cognitive load
Making next actions obvious
Reducing dependency on activity history
Helping agents understand pending work instantly
Improving adoption among agents currently working on Excel sheets

The redesign should be non-destructive and easily reversible.

Change 1: Keep Stage Bar But Make It Secondary

Current:

NEW → CONTACTED → QUOTE → PAYMENT DONE → POLICY

Keep this exactly as is.

Do not change the state machine.

Do not remove bucket navigation.

However, treat the stage bar as informational.

The stage bar should not be the primary thing an agent interacts with.

Change 2: Add "Lead Action Center" Below Stage Bar

Directly below the stage bar add a compact card.

This card should always answer:

What is happening?
What is pending?
What should I do next?

Layout:

Current Status:
Quote Shared

Sub Status:
Exploring Options

Pending With:
Customer

Follow-up:
25 Jun 2026

Next Recommended Action:
Follow up and confirm selected insurer.

This becomes the most important card on the screen.

Change 3: Add "Lead Health Widget"

Display a small summary card.

Example:

Lead Health

Stage:
Quote

Last Activity:
2 hrs ago

Pending Since:
1 Day

Pending With:
Customer

Risk:
Medium

Risk logic:

Low

Activity within 2 days

Medium

No activity for 3-5 days

High

No activity for 5+ days

This helps managers and agents prioritize.

Change 4: Convert Application Data Into Progress Tracker

Current left panel:

Insurance Details
Customer Details
Income Details
Property Details
Nominee Details
Health Screening

Add completion indicators.

Example:

✓ Insurance Details

✓ Customer Details

⚠ Income Details Missing

⚠ Property Details Missing

✓ Nominee Details

✓ Health Screening

The agent should instantly know what information is 
<truncated 1475 bytes>
roduct.

Credit Life
✓ Payment Verified

✓ Documents Received

○ Medical Scheduled

○ Medical Completed

○ Underwriting

○ Approval

○ Policy Issued
Property Insurance
✓ Payment Verified

○ KYC Pending

○ KYC Completed

○ Policy Issued
Change 8: Add Follow-up Widget

Current follow-ups are hidden inside status updates.

Add dedicated widget.

Example:

Upcoming Follow-up

25 Jun 2026

Pending With:
Customer

Reason:
Exploring Options

This should always be visible.

Change 9: Improve Activity History

Current activity history is too generic.

Group activities.

Example:

Status Updates

Quote Shared
Payment Link Shared

--------------------------------

Customer Communication

WhatsApp Sent
Call Connected

--------------------------------

Documents

Payment Proof Uploaded
Policy Copy Uploaded

This makes history easier to scan.

Change 10: Add Sticky Summary Bar

When scrolling, keep a compact sticky summary.

Example:

Priya Sharma

Loan Protection

Quote Stage

Pending With Customer

Follow-up Tomorrow

Agents should never lose context while scrolling.

What Not To Change

Do not change:

State machine
Buckets
Statuses
Sub-statuses
Dashboard metrics
Top summary cards

Those are already good.

The issue is not the data model.

The issue is helping agents understand:

What should I do next?

If you implement only the Action Center, Processing Checklist, Missing Information Indicators, and Follow-up Widget, adoption will improve significantly without rebuilding the CRM. Those four changes alone will solve most of the usability concerns raised by your managers and tech team.

<USER_REQUEST>
Prompt:
Make the milestone tracker in the Payment Done bucket fully configurable based on the product and insurer selected on the lead. The milestones must not be hardcoded — they must be driven by a configuration object that maps product + insurer to a milestone sequence.

Configuration structure:
Define a single MILESTONE_CONFIG object at the top of the component. All milestone sequences are defined here. The tracker reads from this config — never hardcoded inline.
javascriptconst MILESTONE_CONFIG = {
  'loan_protection_care': {
    label: 'Loan Protection · CARE Health',
    milestones: [
      { id: 'payment_verified',       label: 'Payment Verified',       completable: false },
      { id: 'proposal_form_pending',  label: 'Proposal Form Pending',  completable: true,  nextLabel: 'Mark as Proposal Form Completed' },
      { id: 'proposal_form_completed',label: 'Proposal Form Completed',completable: true,  nextLabel: 'Mark Ready for Policy' },
      { id: 'policy_copy_upload',     label: 'Policy Copy Upload',     completable: false, isUpload: true },
    ]
  },
  'loan_protection_tata': {
    label: 'Loan Protection · TATA AIG',
    milestones: [
      { id: 'payment_verified', label: 'Payment Verified',  completable: false },
      { id: 'tele_pd_pending',  label: 'Tele-PD Pending',   completable: true, nextLabel: 'Mark as Tele-PD Completed' },
      { id: 'tele_pd_completed',label: 'Tele-PD Completed', completable: true, nextLabel: 'Mark Ready for Policy' },
      { id: 'policy_copy_upload',label: 'Policy Copy Upload', completable: false, isUpload: true },
    ]
  },
  'property_insurance': {
    label: 'Property Insurance',
    milestones: [
      { id: 'payment_verified', label: 'Payment Verified',  completable: false },
      { id: 'kyc_pending',      label: 'KYC Pending',       completable: true, nextLabel: 'Mark as KYC Completed' },
      { id: 'kyc_completed',    label: 'KYC Completed',     completable: true, nextLabel: 'Mark Ready for Policy' },
      { id: 'policy_copy_upload',lab
<truncated 1553 bytes>
olicy Decision' },
      { id: 'policy_decision',    label: 'Policy Decision',    completable: false, isDecision: true },
      { id: 'policy_copy_upload', label: 'Policy Copy Upload', completable: false, isUpload: true },
    ]
  }
}

How the tracker reads the config:
The lead record has two fields: product_type and insurer. These two together determine which config key to use:
javascriptfunction getMilestoneKey(product, insurer) {
  if (product === 'loan_protection') {
    return insurer?.toLowerCase().includes('care') 
      ? 'loan_protection_care' 
      : 'loan_protection_tata';
  }
  if (product === 'property_insurance') return 'property_insurance';
  if (product === 'credit_life')        return 'credit_life';
  if (product === 'term_plan')          return 'term_plan';
}
The tracker component takes milestoneKey as its only prop and reads everything — label, milestone sequence, button labels, special flags — from MILESTONE_CONFIG[milestoneKey].

Special milestone flags:
Each milestone node in the config can have these flags:

completable: true — shows the "Mark as [next]" action button on the active milestone
completable: false — no action button (Payment Verified is already done; Policy Copy Upload has its own upload UI)
isUpload: true — triggers Section 3 (Policy Copy Upload card) to appear instead of a regular action button
isDecision: true — triggers the 3-option decision pills (Approved / Counter Offer / Rejected) instead of a regular action button


Adding new products or insurers in future:
To add a new insurer or product milestone track in future — only MILESTONE_CONFIG needs updating. No changes to the tracker component itself. This makes it fully extensible without touching core logic.

No visual changes. The milestone tracker looks exactly the same. This change is purely architectural — making the data-driven so any future product or insurer can be added in one place.
</USER_REQUEST>

<USER_REQUEST>
Prompt:
Fix two stage-transition bugs introduced by the accordion restructuring.

Bug 1 — Stage bar and center panel content mismatch
Currently the stage bar shows "Contacted" as active while the center panel renders QUOTE bucket content (Shared Quotes / Share Payment Link / Customer Selected). This means the lead's actual current_stage value was never updated to "quote" when the agent shared a quote earlier, even though the UI moved forward visually.
Root cause to fix: The stage bar's active state and the center panel's rendered content must both read from the SAME single source of truth — lead.current_stage. There cannot be two separate variables tracking "what stage to show in the bar" vs "what content to show in the panel." Audit the state management:

When "Share Quote" / "Share All Quotes" is clicked in the Contacted accordion section → this must set lead.current_stage = 'quote' in the actual lead state object, not just visually swap the rendered component
The stage bar component reads lead.current_stage to determine which chevron is active/done/pending
The center panel component reads the SAME lead.current_stage to determine which section is the "active editable" section at the bottom vs which sections become collapsed accordions above it

Fix: consolidate to one stage value. Every transition action (Generate Quote, Share Quote, Share Payment Link, Mark as Payment Verified, Mark as Policy Copy Received) must update this single lead.current_stage field, and both the stage bar and center panel must re-render from it.

Bug 2 — Sharing payment link does not move lead to Payment Done
When agent clicks "Share Payment Link" inside the Quote bucket Payment card and completes the share action (WhatsApp/Email popup selection):
This action should NOT move the lead to Payment Done yet — that was never correct. Payment Link Shared only updates STATUS to "Payment Link Shared" / SUB STATUS "Awaiting Payment" and the lead REMAINS in Quote bucket. The lead only moves to Payment Done when the separate Payment Verification step is completed and the Manager/Agent clicks "Mark as Verified."
Confirm correct transition map — re-verify this exact logic is implemented:
ActionStage BeforeStage AfterGenerate Quote clicked (NEW)NewContactedShare Quote / Share All clicked (Contacted)ContactedQuoteShare Payment Link clicked (Quote)QuoteQuote (no change — status updates only)Mark as Verified clicked (Quote → Payment Verification)QuotePayment DoneMark as Policy Copy Received clicked (Payment Done)Payment DonePolicy Issued
If the bug was that clicking Share Payment Link incorrectly auto-advanced the stage, remove that incorrect transition. If the bug was that the agent expected it to advance but it's stuck, the actual fix is: agent must complete the Payment Verification section (upload proof → OCR → Mark as Verified) to advance to Payment Done — confirm this flow is fully present and functional below the Payment Link section in the Quote bucket's active (non-collapsed) area.

Testing checklist after fix:

Generate Quote in New → stage bar shows Contacted active, New becomes collapsed accordion
Share Quote in Contacted → stage bar shows Quote active, Contacted becomes collapsed accordion
Customer selection + Share Payment Link in Quote → stage bar STAYS on Quote, no accordion change yet
Upload proof + OCR + Mark as Verified in Quote → stage bar shows Payment Done active, Quote becomes collapsed accordion
Upload Policy Copy + Mark as Policy Copy Received in Payment Done → stage bar shows Policy Issued active, Payment Done becomes collapsed accordion

Each step must persist correctly — refreshing the page or navigating away and back should retain the correct stage and correct accordion states.

Manual status options (agent selects via right panel dropdown, used after calling customer):
javascriptNEW_STATUSES = {

    followUpRequired: true,
    pendingWith: ['Customer']
  },
  'Call Back': {
    subStatuses: ['Customer Busy', 'Not Reachable', 'Switched Off', 'Ringing No Answer', 'Voicemail', 'Customer Disconnected'],
    followUpRequired: true,
    pendingWith: ['Customer']
  },
  'Not Interested': {
    subStatuses: ['Too Expensive', 'Already Insured', 'Not Required', 'Family Not Interested', 'Will Decide Later', 'Other'],
    followUpRequired: false,
    pendingWith: []
  }
}
When followUpRequired: true — Follow-up Date and Pending With fields are shown and mandatory in the right panel. When false — these fields are hidden.
Automatic status trigger (center panel action):
When agent clicks "Generate Quote" (Loan Protection tab) OR "Open PolicyBazaar" (Property/Credit Life/Term tabs) in the NEW bucket:

System auto-sets STATUS = "Interested", SUB STATUS = "Need Quote"
This is NOT shown as a dropdown selection the agent makes — it happens silently in the background
Activity History entry logged: "System Update · Status auto-updated to Interested — Need Quote · Triggered by [Generate Quote / Open PolicyBazaar] action · Just now"
Lead moves to CONTACTED bucket
Right panel "Current Status" bar updates to reflect "Interested · Need Quote"

"Interested" / "Need Quote" does NOT appear as a manually selectable option in the NEW bucket STATUS dropdown — it only ever gets set by this automatic trigger.

Manual status o
<truncated 3072 bytes>
 Pending"
Activity History entry: "Agent Update · [Agent name] · Payment proof submitted for verification · Status auto-updated to Payment Done — Verification Pending · Just now"

General implementation rule across all 3 buckets:
The right panel STATUS dropdown should only show the manually selectable options relevant to that bucket (as defined in the _STATUSES config objects above). Any status/sub-status combination that gets set via an automatic center panel trigger should NOT appear as a selectable option in the dropdown — it only appears in the "Current Status" bar at the top of the right panel after being auto-set, and in the Activity History log.
This prevents the agent from manually selecting "Quote Shared" or "Payment Done — Verified" themselves out of sequence — these only happen as a natural consequence of completing the actual work in the center panel.

<USER_REQUEST>
**Prompt:**

Make the milestone tracker in the Payment Done bucket fully configurable based on the product and insurer selected on the lead. The milestones must not be hardcoded — they must be driven by a configuration object that maps product + insurer to a milestone sequence.

---

**Configuration structure:**

Define a single `MILESTONE_CONFIG` object at the top of the component. All milestone sequences are defined here. The tracker reads from this config — never hardcoded inline.

```javascript
const MILESTONE_CONFIG = {
  'loan_protection_care': {
    label: 'Loan Protection · CARE Health',
    milestones: [
      { id: 'payment_verified',       label: 'Payment Verified',       completable: false },
      { id: 'proposal_form_pending',  label: 'Proposal Form Pending',  completable: true,  nextLabel: 'Mark as Proposal Form Completed' },
      { id: 'proposal_form_completed',label: 'Proposal Form Completed',completable: true,  nextLabel: 'Mark Ready for Policy' },
      { id: 'policy_copy_upload',     label: 'Policy Copy Upload',     completable: false, isUpload: true },
    ]
  },
  'loan_protection_tata': {
    label: 'Loan Protection · TATA AIG',
    milestones: [
      { id: 'payment_verified', label: 'Payment Verified',  completable: false },
      { id: 'tele_pd_pending',  label: 'Tele-PD Pending',   completable: true, nextLabel: 'Mark as Tele-PD Completed' },
      { id: 'tele_pd_completed',label: 'Tele-PD Completed', completable: true, nextLabel: 'Mark Ready for Policy' },
      { id: 'policy_copy_upload',label: 'Policy Copy Upload', completable: false, isUpload: true },
    ]
  },
  'property_insurance': {
    label: 'Property Insurance',
    milestones: [
      { id: 'payment_verified', label: 'Payment Verified',  completable: false },
      { id: 'kyc_pending',      label: 'KYC Pending',       completable: true, nextLabel: 'Mark as KYC Completed' },
      { id: 'kyc_completed',    label: 'KYC Completed',     completable: true, nextLabel: 'Mark Ready for Policy' },
      { id: 'p
<truncated 1652 bytes>
,    completable: false, isDecision: true },
      { id: 'policy_copy_upload', label: 'Policy Copy Upload', completable: false, isUpload: true },
    ]
  }
}
```

---

**How the tracker reads the config:**

The lead record has two fields: `product_type` and `insurer`. These two together determine which config key to use:

```javascript
function getMilestoneKey(product, insurer) {
  if (product === 'loan_protection') {
    return insurer?.toLowerCase().includes('care') 
      ? 'loan_protection_care' 
      : 'loan_protection_tata';
  }
  if (product === 'property_insurance') return 'property_insurance';
  if (product === 'credit_life')        return 'credit_life';
  if (product === 'term_plan')          return 'term_plan';
}
```

The tracker component takes `milestoneKey` as its only prop and reads everything — label, milestone sequence, button labels, special flags — from `MILESTONE_CONFIG[milestoneKey]`.

---

**Special milestone flags:**

Each milestone node in the config can have these flags:
- `completable: true` — shows the "Mark as [next]" action button on the active milestone
- `completable: false` — no action button (Payment Verified is already done; Policy Copy Upload has its own upload UI)
- `isUpload: true` — triggers Section 3 (Policy Copy Upload card) to appear instead of a regular action button
- `isDecision: true` — triggers the 3-option decision pills (Approved / Counter Offer / Rejected) instead of a regular action button

---

**Adding new products or insurers in future:**

To add a new insurer or product milestone track in future — only `MILESTONE_CONFIG` needs updating. No changes to the tracker component itself. This makes it fully extensible without touching core logic.

---

**No visual changes.** The milestone tracker looks exactly the same. This change is purely architectural — making the data-driven so any future product or insurer can be added in one place.
</USER_REQUEST>

**Prompt:**

Make the milestone tracker in the Payment Done bucket fully configurable based on the product and insurer selected on the lead. The milestones must not be hardcoded — they must be driven by a configuration object that maps product + insurer to a milestone sequence.

---

**Configuration structure:**

Define a single `MILESTONE_CONFIG` object at the top of the component. All milestone sequences are defined here. The tracker reads from this config — never hardcoded inline.

```javascript
const MILESTONE_CONFIG = {
  'loan_protection_care': {
    label: 'Loan Protection · CARE Health',
    milestones: [
      { id: 'payment_verified',       label: 'Payment Verified',       completable: false },
      { id: 'proposal_form_pending',  label: 'Proposal Form Pending',  completable: true,  nextLabel: 'Mark as Proposal Form Completed' },
      { id: 'proposal_form_completed',label: 'Proposal Form Completed',completable: true,  nextLabel: 'Mark Ready for Policy' },
      { id: 'policy_copy_upload',     label: 'Policy Copy Upload',     completable: false, isUpload: true },
    ]
  },
  'loan_protection_tata': {
    label: 'Loan Protection · TATA AIG',
    milestones: [
      { id: 'payment_verified', label: 'Payment Verified',  completable: false },
      { id: 'tele_pd_pending',  label: 'Tele-PD Pending',   completable: true, nextLabel: 'Mark as Tele-PD Completed' },
      { id: 'tele_pd_completed',label: 'Tele-PD Completed', completable: true, nextLabel: 'Mark Ready for Policy' },
      { id: 'policy_copy_upload',label: 'Policy Copy Upload', completable: false, isUpload: true },
    ]
  },
  'property_insurance': {
    label: 'Property Insurance',
    milestones: [
      { id: 'payment_verified', label: 'Payment Verified',  completable: false },
      { id: 'kyc_pending',      label: 'KYC Pending',       completable: true, nextLabel: 'Mark as KYC Completed' },
      { id: 'kyc_completed',    label: 'KYC Completed',     completable: true, nextLabel: 'Mark Ready for Policy' },
      { id: 'p
<truncated 1652 bytes>
,    completable: false, isDecision: true },
      { id: 'policy_copy_upload', label: 'Policy Copy Upload', completable: false, isUpload: true },
    ]
  }
}
```

---

**How the tracker reads the config:**

The lead record has two fields: `product_type` and `insurer`. These two together determine which config key to use:

```javascript
function getMilestoneKey(product, insurer) {
  if (product === 'loan_protection') {
    return insurer?.toLowerCase().includes('care') 
      ? 'loan_protection_care' 
      : 'loan_protection_tata';
  }
  if (product === 'property_insurance') return 'property_insurance';
  if (product === 'credit_life')        return 'credit_life';
  if (product === 'term_plan')          return 'term_plan';
}
```

The tracker component takes `milestoneKey` as its only prop and reads everything — label, milestone sequence, button labels, special flags — from `MILESTONE_CONFIG[milestoneKey]`.

---

**Special milestone flags:**

Each milestone node in the config can have these flags:
- `completable: true` — shows the "Mark as [next]" action button on the active milestone
- `completable: false` — no action button (Payment Verified is already done; Policy Copy Upload has its own upload UI)
- `isUpload: true` — triggers Section 3 (Policy Copy Upload card) to appear instead of a regular action button
- `isDecision: true` — triggers the 3-option decision pills (Approved / Counter Offer / Rejected) instead of a regular action button

---

**Adding new products or insurers in future:**

To add a new insurer or product milestone track in future — only `MILESTONE_CONFIG` needs updating. No changes to the tracker component itself. This makes it fully extensible without touching core logic.

---

**No visual changes.** The milestone tracker looks exactly the same. This change is purely architectural — making the data-driven so any future product or insurer can be added in one place.

- Assignee column shows previous agent name (muted, not reassignable until reopened)

- Full page shows the Lead Closed state same as agent view BUT with one additional button below "← Back to Lead List":

- A small inline prompt appears below the button:
  - Label: "REOPEN REASON *" font-size 10px font-weight 700 uppercase color #9CA3AF margin-bottom 6px
  - Text input: full width, height 38px, border 1.5px solid #E5E7EB, border-radius 6px, font-size 12px, placeholder "Why is this lead being reopened?"
  - "Confirm Reopen" button: full width, height 40px, background #473391, color white, border-radius 8px, font-size 13px font-weight 700, margin-top 8px
  - Disabled until reason is typed (min 5 characters)

On confirming reopen:
- Lead moves back to the bucket it was in before being marked Lost
- Lead reappears in IBM Agent's queue (same assignee as before)
- Activity History entry: "IBM Manager · [Manager name] · Lead reopened from Lost · Reason: [reason] · Just now"
- Green toast: "Lead reopened. Returned to [previous bucket] stage."
- Page refreshes to show the lead detail in its restored bucket state

- Left side: small stage icon/dot (colored per stage — purple for New, blue for Contacted, amber for Quote) + stage name font-size 13px font-weight 700 color #111827 + a brief one-line summary in font-size 11px color #6B7280 margin-left 8px
- Right side: chevron icon ▾ that rotates 180° when expanded, color #9CA3AF, transition transform 0.2s

**Expanded content (shown when section is clicked open):**
- Padding 18px, background white, border-top 1px solid #F3F4F6
- Contains the exact same UI that was originally shown in that stage's center panel — but every interactive element is now **read-only / disabled**:
  - Form inputs: background #F9FAFB, border 1px solid #F3F4F6, cursor not-allowed, no focus state
  - Buttons (Generate Quote, Share Quote, Open PolicyBazaar, Share Payment Link etc.): completely removed — only the data/result they produced remains visible
  - Checkboxes/radio/pill toggles: shown in their final selected state, visually muted (opacity 0.7), not clickable
  - Quote cards: show all data (insurer, premium, coverage) but remove Share Quote buttons — replace with a static "Shared" badge if it was shared
  - Tabs (Loan Protection / Property / Credit Life / Term Plan): show only the one that was actually used, no tab switcher

Default state: **all accordion sections start collapsed.**
